                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                      <a href="http://www.stadiumbee.com">
                       StadiumBee - It's Your Game Day, Own it!
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5264600225424843020" itemprop="articleBody">
                      Quarterback Blog followers and fans - please check out my new venture
                      <b>
                       <a href="http://www.stadiumbee.com/" target="_blank">
                        StadiumBee
                       </a>
                       .
                      </b>
                      The mobile app is available for download on iOS and Android.  We're in the early stages of our business but would love your support and feedback.  Please share and spread the word!
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <a href="http://www.stadiumbee.com/" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" target="_blank">
                       <img border="0" data-original-height="900" data-original-width="1600" height="180" src="https://1.bp.blogspot.com/-bX-zLmPfU1w/Wd6WgwCvHqI/AAAAAAAACr8/-rGH8_VFCx0Bopcx20ZcF4aAf_aZNYOywCLcBGAs/s320/20229894_476287986068007_8128426576763828723_o.jpg" width="320"/>
                      </a>
                      What is StadiumBee?  StadiumBee was designed to help fans plan their live sporting event experience.  We provide users with the ability to search and review their favorite venue amenities and sections.  The application also provides users with local 411 favorites (local business like restaurants and parking that reside near the venues).  We're excited about the information we're surfacing for fans and eager to help maximize their overall gameday experience.
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      <ul>
                       <li>
                        <a href="https://appurl.io/j3uggs10" target="_blank">
                         Download for iOS here
                        </a>
                       </li>
                       <li>
                        <a href="https://appurl.io/j3uggs10" target="_blank">
                         Download for Android here
                        </a>
                       </li>
                      </ul>
                      <br/>
                      <b>
                       <span style="font-size: large;">
                        #OwnYourOuting
                       </span>
                      </b>
                      <div style="clear: both;">
                      </div>
                     </div>

                    <div class="post hentry uncustomized-post-template" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                     <meta content="1286799383485367538" itemprop="blogId"/>

                     </a>
                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                      <a href="http://www.thequarterbackblog.com/2014/02/qb-lead-camp-in-philadelphia-pa.html">
                       QB L.E.A.D Camp in Philadelphia, PA
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-73974450872288601" itemprop="articleBody">
                      <div class="MsoNoSpacing">
                       Come take part in the QB L.E.A.D camp that will give you
 a start on your training to take the next step! This camp will give a
 quarterback a great opportunity to learn about, and develop the physical,
 mental and leadership skills necessary in playing the most demanding position
 in sports.
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNoSpacing">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNoSpacing">
                       Drills will concentrate on improving three phases of mechanics (Footwork,
 Throwing and Vision). Classroom session includes video analysis, coverage recognition
 and leadership exercises. Learn the proper techniques and take home tools to
 lead your team to the top.
                       <o:p>
                       </o:p>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNoSpacing">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal">
                       <b>
                        <span style="color: #990000;">
                         WHERE:
                        </span>
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal">
                       St. Joseph’s
 Preparatory School
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal">
                       1733
 W. Girard Ave
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal">
                       Philadelphia,
 PA 19131
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal">
                       <span style="color: #990000;">
                        <b>
                         FOR MORE INFORMATION:
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal">
                       <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                        <b>
                         Contact:
                        </b>
                        Tim Roken
                        <b>
                         <o:p>
                         </o:p>
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal">
                       <span style="font-family: inherit;">
                        Assistant Head
 Coach/Offensive Coordinator St. Joseph’s Prep
                        <b>
                         <o:p>
                         </o:p>
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNormal">

                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-1607046712502828047" itemprop="articleBody">
                      <b>
                       <span style="font-size: large;">
                        Mercer Football
                       </span>
                       <br/>
                       NCAA Record 10 Wins in First Season
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      <br/>
                      Click below for more information, dates and registration:
                      <br/>
                      -
                      <a href="http://www.bobbylambfootballcamp.com/Default.aspx?tabid=21632" target="_blank">
                       2014 Quarterback/Receiver School
                      </a>
                      <br/>

                       2014 Offensive Lineman School
                      </a>

                      </a>

                       2014 Senior Elite Day Camps
                      </a>

                       2014 Youth Skills Camp

                    <div class="post hentry uncustomized-post-template" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">

                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                      <a href="http://www.thequarterbackblog.com/2013/11/whitfield-athletix-qb-coach-george.html">
                       Whitfield Athletix - QB Coach George Whitfield Jr.
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-3821881966347301523" itemprop="articleBody">
                      <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       Train with one of the best quarterback coaches and staff in the country.
                       <span style="background-color: white; line-height: 18px;">
                        Whitfield Athletix is built specifically to train and prepare the skill sets of quarterbacks to succeed through evaluations, testing, and most importantly, defenses.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       <br/>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       <b>
                        Website:
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <a href="http://www.whitfieldqb.com/" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       http://www.whitfieldqb.com
                      </a>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       <b>
                        E-mail:
                       </b>
                      </span>
                      <a href="mailto:WhitfieldQBacademy@gmail.com" style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin: 0px; padding: 0px; text-decoration: none;">
                       WhitfieldQBacademy@gmail.com
                      </a>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                       <span style="margin: 0px; padding: 0px;">
                        <b>
                         Phone:
                        </b>
                        (
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       619) 708-5557
                      </span>

                 <div class="date-outer">
                  <h2 class="date-header">
                   <span>
                    Tuesday, July 16, 2013
                   </span>
                  </h2>
                  <div class="date-posts">
                   <div class="post-outer">
                    <div class="post hentry uncustomized-post-template" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                     <meta content="1286799383485367538" itemprop="blogId"/>
                     <meta content="7432049613226306577" itemprop="postId"/>
                     <a name="7432049613226306577">
                     </a>
                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                      <a href="http://www.thequarterbackblog.com/2013/07/collin-drafts-skills-camp-quarterback.html">
                       Collin Drafts Skills Camp - Quarterback Nation
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-7432049613226306577" itemprop="articleBody">
                      <div style="color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       <span style="background-color: white;">
                        Collin Drafts' Skills Camp, QuarterbackNation's final training camp of the summer, will take place on
                       </span>
                       <span class="aBn" data-term="goog_446103484" style="border-bottom-color: rgb(204, 204, 204); border-bottom-style: dashed; border-bottom-width: 1px; position: relative; top: -2px; z-index: 0;" tabindex="0">
                        <span class="aQJ" style="position: relative; top: 2px; z-index: -1;">
                         July 24th-25th
                        </span>
                       </span>
                       <span style="background-color: white;">
                       </span>
                       <span style="background-color: white;">
                        at West Orange HS. This will be a 2 day camp that will be open to all QB's, WR's, and DB's ages 10 and up.
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       <span style="background-color: white;">
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       <span style="background-color: white;">
                        Each position group will be coached in our 'training progression" process that will breakdown the fundamentals and fine tune the players' ability and understanding of his position. Do not miss the opportunity to get that competitive edge over your opponent before entering into fall training camp. Staff will include current and former NFL, CFL, AFL and current members of the Orlando Predators football team.
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       To register visit -
                       <a href="http://www.quarterbacknation.com/drafts-skills-camp/" style="color: #1155cc;" target="_blank">
                        http://www.
                        <wbr>
                        </wbr>
                        quarterbacknation.com/drafts-
                        <wbr>
                        </wbr>
                        skills-camp
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       Preregistration is $100. Walk ups at the first day of the event will be $125. ***All positions must pay*** This is not just a QB camp, as each position will receive the same intense individual coaching.
                      </div>
                      <div style="clear: both;">
                      </div>
                     </div>

                     </a>
                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                      <a href="http://www.thequarterbackblog.com/2013/05/check-out-qb-fraternity-by-chris-malleo.html">
                       Check Out The QB Fraternity, by Chris Malleo
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-5374374537196590628" itemprop="articleBody">
                      <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       The QB Fraternity was
 founded by Chris Malleo. Chris was the NJ high school Offensive Player of the
 Year in 2002.  He went on to become one of the most versatile players in
 the history of Northwestern University Football. He then went on to play football
 in the Arena and Canadian Football leagues.
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       <br/>
                      </span>
                      <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       Today he serves as the assistant
 Head Coach and Quarterbacks Coach for the nationally ranked Lawrenceville
 School. He also is one of the top private quarterback tutors in the country. If
 you need to contact Chris for lessons, comments, or suggestions please see
 the
                      </span>
                      <a href="http://www.theqbfraternity.com/pages/contact-us" style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;" title="contact us">
                       <span style="background-color: white; background-position: initial initial; background-repeat: initial initial; border: 1pt none windowtext; color: #4a7491; padding: 0in; text-decoration: none;">
                        contact
 us
                       </span>
                      </a>
                      <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       page.
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       <br/>
                      </span>
                      <a href="http://www.theqbfraternity.com/" style="background-color: white; font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif; line-height: 27.1875px;">
                       <b>
                        www.theqbfraternity.com
                       </b>
                      </a>
                      <div style="clear: both;">
                      </div>
                     </div>

                      </a>
                     </h3>

                      <div class="post-header-line-1">

                       <u>
                        <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">

                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                      <a href="http://www.thequarterbackblog.com/2013/03/elite-quarterback-camps-with-ty-detmer.html">
                       Elite Quarterback Camps with Ty Detmer
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-7687625516321532700" itemprop="articleBody">
                      <b style="color: #222222;">
                       <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                        QB Elite 2-Day Quarterback and Receiver Camp
                       </span>
                      </b>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="background-color: white; color: #222222;">
                       <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                        July 5th - July 6th -- Salt Lake City, Utah
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="background-color: white; color: #222222;">
                       <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span style="background-color: white; color: #222222;">
                       <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                        Join former Heisman Trophy Winner and 15 year NFL veteran Ty Detmer and experienced quarterback coach Dustin Smith.
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="background-color: white; color: #222222;">
                       <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                      </span>
                      <span style="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, sans-serif;">
                       <span style="background-color: white; color: #222222;">
                        Visit
                       </span>
                       <a href="http://www.qbelite.com/" style="background-color: white; color: #1155cc;" target="_blank">
                        www.QBelite.com
                       </a>
                       <span style="background-color: white; color: #222222;">
                        for more information or sign up
                        <a href="http://www.qbelite.com/camp-signup.html" target="_blank">
                         here
                        </a>
                        .

                   <span>
                    Saturday, February 23, 2013
                   </span>
                  </h2>
                  <div class="date-posts">
                   <div class="post-outer">
                    <div class="post hentry uncustomized-post-template" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                     <meta content="1286799383485367538" itemprop="blogId"/>
                     <meta content="4934696753177068947" itemprop="postId"/>
                     <a name="4934696753177068947">
                     </a>
                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                      <a href="http://www.thequarterbackblog.com/2013/02/perfect-performance-quarterback-training.html">
                       Perfect Performance - Quarterback Training
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-4934696753177068947" itemprop="articleBody">
                      <span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       Perfect Performance is a full service sports performance training
                      </span>
                      <span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       center located in the Washington DC Metro Area.  Perfect Performance serves athletes in Maryland, DC and Northern Virginia.
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       <br/>
                      </span>
                      <span style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       The QB Academy is designed to develop QB's from ages 8 to professional level.  There are currently 3 QB coaches on staff; Bryson Spinner, Sean Glennon and Eddie McGee.
                      </span>
                      <br/>
                      <div style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       <br/>
                      </div>
                      <div style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       <b>
                        Perfect Performance
                       </b>
                      </div>
                      <div style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       <a href="http://www.perfect-performance.com/" style="color: #1155cc;" target="_blank">
                        www.perfect-performance.com
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div style="background-color: white; color: #222222; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13px;">
                       <a href="tel:703-539-2385" style="color: #1155cc;" target="_blank" value="+17035392385">
                        703-539-2385
                       </a>

                       <u>

                       </u>
                      </b>
                      <br/>

                      </b>

                 <div class="date-outer">
                  <h2 class="date-header">
                   <span>
                    Thursday, December 27, 2012
                   </span>
                  </h2>
                  <div class="date-posts">
                   <div class="post-outer">
                    <div class="post hentry uncustomized-post-template" itemprop="blogPost" itemscope="itemscope" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
                     <meta content="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-7spvzNf38qo/UNycKuRnTXI/AAAAAAAAAqc/SoCgLQVcnsk/s400/header_1.png" itemprop="image_url"/>
                     <meta content="1286799383485367538" itemprop="blogId"/>
                     <meta content="1866690964612942208" itemprop="postId"/>
                     <a name="1866690964612942208">
                     </a>
                     <h3 class="post-title entry-title" itemprop="name">
                      <a href="http://www.thequarterbackblog.com/2012/12/bobby-lamb-quarterback-and-receiver.html">
                       Bobby Lamb Quarterback and Receiver School
                      </a>
                     </h3>
                     <div class="post-header">
                      <div class="post-header-line-1">
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-1866690964612942208" itemprop="articleBody">
                      <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                       <a href="http://www.bobbylambfootballcamp.com/" target="_blank">
                        <img border="0" height="80" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-7spvzNf38qo/UNycKuRnTXI/AAAAAAAAAqc/SoCgLQVcnsk/s400/header_1.png" width="400"/>
                       </a>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNoSpacing">
                       <span style="background: white;">
                        <b>
                         <br/>
                        </b>
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="text-align: center;">
                       <b>
                        <a href="http://www.bobbylambfootballcamp.com/" style="color: #1155cc; font-family: arial, sans-serif; font-size: 13.333333969116211px;" target="_blank">
                         http://www.
                         <wbr>
                         </wbr>
                         bobbylambfootballcamp.com
                        </a>
                       </b>
                       - Macon, Georgia
                       <br/>
                       <span style="background-color: white; text-align: left;">
                        <br/>
                       </span>
                       <div style="text-align: justify;">
                        <span style="background-color: white; text-align: left;">
                         The
                        </span>
                        <b style="text-align: left;">
                         Bobby Lamb Quarterback
 and Receiver School
                        </b>
                        <span style="background-color: white; text-align: left;">
                         is intended to offer a unique learning experience where
 teaching is emphasized and individual improvement is the goal. This camp gives
 participants maximum drill repetition enhanced by lectures, video, and film
 study. Participants will be grouped by grade level and position. Quarterbacks and
 receivers from the same school will be paired so that they can work together in
 appropriate drills.
                        </span>
                       </div>
                       <span style="background-color: white;">
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div class="MsoNoSpacing">
                       <div style="text-align: left;">
                        <br/>
                       </div>
                       <b>
                        <u>
                         <span style="background: white;">
                          Program of Instruction Includes:
                         </span>
                        </u>
                       </b>
                       <br/>
                       <span style="background: white;">
                        Mechanics/fundamentals of passing: footwork, balance, drops,
 passing from a set position, ball handling techniques, option fundamentals,
 coverage recognition, throwing routes (out, curl, etc.), goal line passes, film
 study of techniques and coverage, video study of individual technique, methods
 to improve quickness and speed.
                       </span>
                      </div>
                      <div style="clear: both;">
                      </div>
                     </div>
                     <div class="post-footer">

                 <h2 class="title">
                  Welcome to The Quarterback Blog
                 </h2>
                 <div class="widget-content">
                  <p class="MsoNormal">
                   Success at quarterback starts with a determination to be the best and a work ethic to make it happen.  The Quarterback Blog was created to break out crucial fundamentals into quick and easy to understand skill guides for quarterbacks and coaches.  New skill guides will be added regularly.
                   <br/>
                  </p>
                  <p class="MsoNormal">
                   <span class="Apple-style-span">
                    <b>
                     Quarterback Coaches:
                    </b>
                    <br/>
                    Send over your contact information and we will add you to the quarterback coach directory, free of charge.
                   </span>
                  </p>
                  <p class="MsoNormal" style="color:#990000;">
                   <span style="font-style: italic;">
                    "The difference between a successful person and the others is not a lack of strength or knowledge but rather a lack of will."
                   </span>
                   - Vince Lombardi
                  </p>
                  <ul style="background-color: white; line-height: 1.2; margin: 0px; padding: 0px 0px 0px 1.25em;font-family:Arial, Tahoma, Helvetica, FreeSans, sans-serif;font-size:12px;color:#222222;">
                   <li style="margin: 0px; padding: 0.25em 0px;">
                    <span style="color:#0b5394;">
                     <a href="http://www.thequarterbackblog.com/p/advertise-on-quarterback-blog.html">
                      Advertise on The Quarterback Blog
                     </a>
                    </span>
                   </li>

                   </li>
